\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{MP3\ audio\ decoder.\ Choice\ of\ public\ domain\ or\ MIT-\/0.\ See\ license\ statements\ at\ the\ end\ of\ this\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{dr\_mp3\ -\/\ v0.4.7\ -\/\ 2019-\/07-\/28}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{David\ Reid\ -\/\ mackron@gmail.com}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{Based\ off\ minimp3\ (https://github.com/lieff/minimp3)\ which\ is\ where\ the\ real\ work\ was\ done.\ See\ the\ bottom\ of\ this\ file\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{differences\ between\ minimp3\ and\ dr\_mp3.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{USAGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{=====}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{dr\_mp3\ is\ a\ single-\/file\ library.\ To\ use\ it,\ do\ something\ like\ the\ following\ in\ one\ .c\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#define\ DR\_MP3\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \#include\ "{}dr\_mp3.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ then\ \#include\ this\ file\ in\ other\ parts\ of\ the\ program\ as\ you\ would\ with\ any\ other\ header\ file.\ To\ decode\ audio\ data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{do\ something\ like\ the\ following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\ mp3;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ if\ (!drmp3\_init\_file(\&mp3,\ "{}MySong.mp3"{},\ NULL))\ \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Failed\ to\ open\ file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_uint64\ framesRead\ =\ drmp3\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32(pMP3,\ framesToRead,\ pFrames);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ drmp3\ object\ is\ transparent\ so\ you\ can\ get\ access\ to\ the\ channel\ count\ and\ sample\ rate\ like\ so:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_uint32\ channels\ =\ mp3.channels;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ drmp3\_uint32\ sampleRate\ =\ mp3.sampleRate;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ third\ parameter\ of\ drmp3\_init\_file()\ in\ the\ example\ above\ allows\ you\ to\ control\ the\ output\ channel\ count\ and\ sample\ rate.\ It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{is\ a\ pointer\ to\ a\ drmp3\_config\ object.\ Setting\ any\ of\ the\ variables\ of\ this\ object\ to\ 0\ will\ cause\ dr\_mp3\ to\ use\ defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{The\ example\ above\ initializes\ a\ decoder\ from\ a\ file,\ but\ you\ can\ also\ initialize\ it\ from\ a\ block\ of\ memory\ and\ read\ and\ seek}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{callbacks\ with\ drmp3\_init\_memory()\ and\ drmp3\_init()\ respectively.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ do\ not\ need\ to\ do\ any\ annoying\ memory\ management\ when\ reading\ PCM\ frames\ -\/\ this\ is\ all\ managed\ internally.\ You\ can\ request}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00042\ \textcolor{comment}{any\ number\ of\ PCM\ frames\ in\ each\ call\ to\ drmp3\_read\_pcm\_frames\_f32()\ and\ it\ will\ return\ as\ many\ PCM\ frames\ as\ it\ can,\ up\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00043\ \textcolor{comment}{requested\ amount.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00044\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{You\ can\ also\ decode\ an\ entire\ file\ in\ one\ go\ with\ drmp3\_open\_and\_read\_f32(),\ drmp3\_open\_memory\_and\_read\_f32()\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{drmp3\_open\_file\_and\_read\_f32().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{OPTIONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{=======}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ these\ options\ before\ including\ this\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ DR\_MP3\_NO\_STDIO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Disable\ drmp3\_init\_file(),\ etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\#define\ DR\_MP3\_NO\_SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ Disable\ SIMD\ optimizations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{03794\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03795\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03796\ \textcolor{comment}{DIFFERENCES\ BETWEEN\ minimp3\ AND\ dr\_mp3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03797\ \textcolor{comment}{======================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03798\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ First,\ keep\ in\ mind\ that\ minimp3\ (https://github.com/lieff/minimp3)\ is\ where\ all\ the\ real\ work\ was\ done.\ All\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03799\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ code\ relating\ to\ the\ actual\ decoding\ remains\ mostly\ unmodified,\ apart\ from\ some\ namespacing\ changes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03800\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_mp3\ adds\ a\ pulling\ style\ API\ which\ allows\ you\ to\ deliver\ raw\ data\ via\ callbacks.\ So,\ rather\ than\ pushing\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03801\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ to\ the\ decoder,\ the\ decoder\ \_pulls\_\ data\ from\ your\ callbacks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03802\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ In\ addition\ to\ callbacks,\ a\ decoder\ can\ be\ initialized\ from\ a\ block\ of\ memory\ and\ a\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03803\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ The\ dr\_mp3\ pull\ API\ reads\ PCM\ frames\ rather\ than\ whole\ MP3\ frames.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03804\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_mp3\ adds\ convenience\ APIs\ for\ opening\ and\ decoding\ entire\ files\ in\ one\ go.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03805\ \textcolor{comment}{-\/\ dr\_mp3\ is\ fully\ namespaced,\ including\ the\ implementation\ section,\ which\ is\ more\ suitable\ when\ compiling\ projects}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03806\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ as\ a\ single\ translation\ unit\ (aka\ unity\ builds).\ At\ the\ time\ of\ writing\ this,\ a\ unity\ build\ is\ not\ possible\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03807\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ using\ minimp3\ in\ conjunction\ with\ stb\_vorbis.\ dr\_mp3\ addresses\ this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03808\ \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03809\ }
